import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

CPP_SOURCE = r"""
void attn_from_qkv_forward(torch::Tensor,torch::Tensor,int,int,int,int);
"""

CUDA_SOURCE = r"""
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <torch/extension.h>

__global__ void attn_from_qkv_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ qkv,
    float* __restrict__ out,
    int B_outer, int L, int D, int num_heads
) {
    int b = blockIdx.x;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    int head_dim = D / num_heads;

    extern __shared__ float smem[];
    float* s_qkv = smem;
    float* s_out = smem + L * 3 * D;

    const float* qkv_ptr = qkv + b * L * 3 * D;

    for (int i = tid; i < L * 3 * D; i += blockDim.x)
        s_qkv[i] = qkv_ptr[i];
    __syncthreads();

    int head = tid / L;
    int pos = tid % L;

    if (head < num_heads) {
        float q_reg[16];
        for (int d = 0; d < head_dim; d++)
            q_reg[d] = s_qkv[pos * 3 * D + head * head_dim + d];

        float scores[32];
        float max_sc = -1e30f;
        for (int kpos = 0; kpos < L; kpos++) {
            float dot = 0.0f;
            for (int d = 0; d < head_dim; d++)
                dot += q_reg[d] * s_qkv[kpos * 3 * D + D + head * head_dim + d];
            dot *= rsqrtf((float)head_dim);
            scores[kpos] = dot;
            max_sc = fmaxf(max_sc, dot);
        }

        float sum_exp = 0.0f;
        for (int kpos = 0; kpos < L; kpos++) {
            scores[kpos] = expf(scores[kpos] - max_sc);
            sum_exp += scores[kpos];
        }
        float isum = 1.0f / sum_exp;

        for (int d = 0; d < head_dim; d++) {
            float acc = 0.0f;
            for (int kpos = 0; kpos < L; kpos++)
                acc += scores[kpos] * s_qkv[kpos * 3 * D + 2 * D + head * head_dim + d];
            s_out[pos * D + head * head_dim + d] = acc * isum;
        }
    }
    __syncthreads();

    float* out_ptr = out + b * L * D;
    for (int i = tid; i < L * D; i += blockDim.x)
        out_ptr[i] = s_out[i];
}

void attn_from_qkv_forward(
    torch::Tensor qkv,
    torch::Tensor out,
    int B_outer, int L, int D, int num_heads
) {
    dim3 grid(B_outer);
    dim3 block(128);
    size_t smem_size = (L * 3 * D + L * D) * sizeof(float);
    attn_from_qkv_kernel<<<grid, block, smem_size>>>(
        qkv.data_ptr<float>(),
        out.data_ptr<float>(),
        B_outer, L, D, num_heads
    );
}
"""

_cuda_ext = load_inline(
    name="axial_attn_hybrid_v1",
    cpp_sources=CPP_SOURCE,
    cuda_sources=CUDA_SOURCE,
    functions=["attn_from_qkv_forward"],
    extra_cuda_cflags=["-O3", "--expt-relaxed-constexpr"],
)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, dim, num_heads, height, width, dropout=0.0):
        super().__init__()
        self.height = height
        self.width = width
        self.num_heads = num_heads
        self.head_dim = dim // num_heads
        assert dim % num_heads == 0

        self.row_norm = nn.LayerNorm(dim)
        self.row_qkv = nn.Linear(dim, 3 * dim, bias=False)
        self.row_out = nn.Linear(dim, dim)

        self.col_norm = nn.LayerNorm(dim)
        self.col_qkv = nn.Linear(dim, 3 * dim, bias=False)
        self.col_out = nn.Linear(dim, dim)

        self.dropout = nn.Dropout(dropout)

    def forward(self, x):
        B, H, W, D = x.shape
        
        # Row-wise attention
        x_row = x.reshape(B * H, W, D)
        x_norm = self.row_norm(x_row)
        qkv = self.row_qkv(x_norm)
        attn_out = torch.empty(B * H, W, D, device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        _cuda_ext.attn_from_qkv_forward(qkv, attn_out, B * H, W, D, self.num_heads)
        x = x + self.row_out(attn_out).reshape(B, H, W, D)

        # Column-wise attention
        x_col = x.permute(0, 2, 1, 3).reshape(B * W, H, D)
        x_norm = self.col_norm(x_col)
        qkv = self.col_qkv(x_norm)
        attn_out = torch.empty(B * W, H, D, device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        _cuda_ext.attn_from_qkv_forward(qkv, attn_out, B * W, H, D, self.num_heads)
        x = x + self.col_out(attn_out).reshape(B, W, H, D).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)

        return x
